<s> a screen and a luxurious couch an the fireplace side stage left <\s>
<s> a door rather right of centre back opening inwards <\s>
<s> a french window right forward a writing table right back <\s>
<s> chloe in a tea gown is standing by the forward end of the sofa very still and very pale <\s>
<s> her lips are parted and her large eyes stare straight before them as if seeing ghosts the door is opened noiselessly and a woman's face is seen <\s>
<s> it peers at chloe vanishes and the door is closed <\s>
<s> chloe raises her hands covers her eyes with them drops them with a quick gesture and looks round her <\s>
<s> with a swift movement she slides on to the sofa and lies prostrate with eyes closed <\s>
